But on the Ctrip booking page, it was written as a twin room, and the front desk did not inform me in advance when checking in. I communicated with the front desk by phone to change the room and was informed that there were no other rooms. The staff "guaranteed" that the door could not be opened.
Let alone the hotel facilities and privacy are ensured by the verbal guarantee of the staff. If the room is two rooms that are connected, shouldn't consumers be informed in advance? Must they be forced to accept it after checking in? Is it a deception that the room type does not match the booking information! Is this how the hotel is managed? If it is not discovered or reported by the guests, it is defaulted?
The room staff said that they would compensate for two breakfasts, but we did not need the hotel's breakfast in our itinerary, and we told the hotel that we would not accept this method. The hotel said that there was no way. After leaving the hotel, someone from the hotel called me and asked if I had any comments and requests. I will deal with it after the trip. What else can I ask for? I feel helpless.
In addition, when I booked on Ctrip, it showed that I could check out late until 2pm. When I checked in, I confirmed the check-out time with the front desk. The staff said that I could apply for membership and then check out late until 2pm. They gave me a form to fill in the information. I explained again that when I booked, Ctrip members already had information about late check-out until 2pm. I didn't need to fill in this form again, right? The front desk still asked me to write my email address and said they would help me register. I was pushed to register as a member. The experience was also very poor.
There were also several signs in the room, and the content confused me. I only took a picture of the one for toiletries. The overall feeling was very inconsistent with the rating of the hotel.
